What Ever Happened to Mitt Romney?

"+ "

It's an age-old question without a very good answer. The man has been basically missing since his loss in the 2008 election against Joe Lieberman. Nowadays, you'll have people online asking how bad Romney, the Governor of Utah, must have been to lose against a man as historically reviled and unpopular as Lieberman was.

The most popular explanation now is that his connections to the unpopular 2007-2009 Republican Congress, that were also taken out during this wave election, were simply too much to bear for the American voter. This could very well be true, since even after 2008 Republican leadership were punished for their attempts to impeach President Gore during that session.

Another answer that you'll likely see a lot is the capture and execution of Osama bin Laden, the mastermind behind 9/11. This seems quite obvious, since it took out a major problem for the Gore administration and allowed Lieberman to pressure Romney for his previously weak support for even looking for Bin Laden.

"+ "

Back to our main question. What ever happened to Mitt Romney?

This started as a meme back in June 2009 when it seemed as if Romney had dropped off the face of the planet, only doing a total of two public interviews between Lieberman's inauguration and the summer. There would go on to be a few more sightings as the meme spread, and online forums of \"Romney Spotters\" cropped to find the elusive man.

Then something happened... he disappeared.

"+ "

The official story, according to his son, Tagg, is that his father traveled across the country to Boston for a business meeting, and then simply never returned home. His business partners in Boston claim he never even showed up. His plane made it to Logan Airport, and he was almost certainly on it, but he never made it to the meeting.

Some more conspiracy-addled minds have claimed that Romney was kidnapped or even murdered on his way between the airport and where the business meeting would occur, but the time frame doesn't make much sense, and it was broad daylight when he landed.

The accepted theory, and the one supported by the Romney family, is that he fled of his own accord. Ann Romney, the former First Lady of Utah, has claimed to have contacted her husband at least once since he went missing, and is sure he is in good health.

"+ "

Wherever Mitt Romney truly is, we may never know, but he will always live on in our hearts as an early meme of the modern era, and a staple of internet culture.
